Below is the duration of execution of 1024 Mandelbrot Set Tasks (class : task.MandelbrotSetTask) which were queued by a client.

No. of registered local computers in the compute space : 2
Computers : Different VMs, same machine
Compute space : Different VM, same machine
Client : Different VM, same machine

For each task, we have noted the following :

* Client Start time (epoch) -> Time at which client submitted the task to the compute space
* Client End time (epoch) -> Time at which client received the result of the task from the compute space
* Client Elapsed time -> Difference between Client start and end times

* Computer Start time -> Time at which task commenced execution in the Computer
* Computer End time -> Time at which Computer produced the result for the task
* Computer Elapsed time -> Difference between Computer start and end times

* Client Total time -> Total time taken to complete all tasks as noted by client
* Client Average time -> Average time taken to complete all tasks as noted by client

* Computer Total time -> Total time taken to complete all tasks as noted by computer
* Computer Average time -> Average time taken to complete all tasks as noted by computer
